<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светиться.html>светя́щийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetjáščijsja</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светиться.html>свети́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светиться.html>светя́щийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetjáščijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>luminous, lambent, lucent</li>
<li>luminescent</li>
<li>radiant</li>
<li>fluorescent</li>
<li>phosphorescent</li>
<li>candescent</li>
<li>agleam</li>
<li>alight <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">lit.: on fire, switched on</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>irradiant</li></ol>

***свеча.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a> (3041)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свѣча</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svěča</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">candle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svěťa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">candle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*světъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ja</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svečá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свечи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>све́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свече́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>candle (a light source, usually of wax)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Svečá</b> goréla na stolé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>A candle</b> was burning on the table.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>све́чи</a></b> - <a href = vnd.unilang:искусственный.html>иску́сственные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:источник.html>исто́чники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Svéči</b> - iskússtvennyje istóčniki svéta.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Candles</b> are artificial light sources.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> candela (unit of luminous intensity)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automotive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spark plug / sparking plug</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> suppository</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">candela</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">канде́ла</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kandɛ́la</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свечение.html>свече́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svečénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свечение.html>свече́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свечение.html>свече́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свечение.html>свече́ний</a></b>)

***свидетель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́тель</a> (1975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съвѣдѣтель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭvědětelĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally contained the archaic root <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вѣд-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">věd-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; after regular dissimilation ѣ-ѣ gt; и-ѣ reanalysed as containing the root <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вид-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vid-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vídetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svidételʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельница.html>свиде́тельница</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>eyewitness, witness (one who has a personal knowledge of something)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svidételʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельство.html>свиде́тельство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svidételʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельство.html>свиде́тельства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельство.html>свиде́тельства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельство.html>свиде́тельств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>evidence, testimony <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">facts presented in support of an assertion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>evidence, illustration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">proof</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>certificate</li></ol>

***свидетельствовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельствовать.html>свиде́тельствовать</a> (3635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельство.html>свиде́тельство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svidételʹstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельствовать.html>свиде́тельствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svidételʹstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">освиде́тельствовать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:засвидетельствовать.html>засвиде́тельствовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to testify, to witness, to be evidence (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свидетельствовать.html>свиде́тельствовать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svidételʹstvovatʹ</b> o čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be evidence of something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***свинство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нство</a> (17932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svínstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> swinishness, rudeness</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dirtiness, flagrant untidiness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нство</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:развести.html>развели́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хне</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kakóje <b>svínstvo</b> oní razvelí na kúxne!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">what a pigpen/pigsty they made out of the kitchen!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meanness, mean/base nature</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mean/low-down trick
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любопытство.html>любопы́тство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>порок</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинство.html>сви́нство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljubopýtstvo ne porok, no bolʹšóje svínstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">curiosity is no disgrace but it is a great inconvenience</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***свинья.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свинья́</a> (2814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svinьja</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sū-</i>. Compare German Schwein.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свинья́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svinʹjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свиньи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>сви́ньи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свине́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pig, hog, sow, swine (mammal of genus <i>Sus</i>)</li></ol>

***свирель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>свирель</a> (31555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свирѣль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svirělĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svirělь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svirati</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ělь</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to buzz, hum</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>свире́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svirélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свирель.html>свире́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свирель.html>свире́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свирель.html>свире́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pipe, svirel <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">musical instrument</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свирепеть.html>свирепе́ть</a> (27644)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свирепый.html>свире́пый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svirépyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свирепеть.html>свирепе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svirepétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассвирепеть.html>рассвирепе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow furious, to begin to see red</li>
<li>to become fierce, to become ferocious, to become cruel</li></ol>

***свирепый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свирепый.html>свирепый</a> (6406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svirěpъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свирепый.html>свире́пый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svirépyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bloodthirsty, ferocious, savage</li>
<li>fierce, furious</li>
<li>wicked, atrocious, savage</li></ol>

***свисать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свисать.html>свиса́ть</a> (5908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сви́снуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svísnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свисать.html>свиса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сви́снуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to droop, to hang down, to dangle
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матренин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:облегать.html>облега́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>густы́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:непрерывный.html>непреры́вные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бакен.html>ба́кены</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выказывать.html>выка́зывая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:подниматься.html>поднима́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:космы.html>ко́смам</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свисавший.html>свиса́вшим</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:темень.html>те́мени</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsjó licó jevó oblegáli gustýje čórnyje vólosy, i neprerývnyje bákeny čórnyje, jedvá vykázyvaja úši, podnimálisʹ k čórnym kósmam, <b>svisávšim</b> s témeni</i></dd><dd>all his face was covered in thick blackhair and swarty sideburns, hiding almost the ears, uninterruptedly rose to the mop which <b>dangled</b> from his [head]crown</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to slouch</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свистать.html>свиста́ть</a> (27282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистнуть.html>сви́стнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svístnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистать.html>свиста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svistátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистнуть.html>сви́стнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whistle, to make a whistling sound <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">without the aid of a whistle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистеть.html>свисте́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svistétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to call someone by whistling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat strongly with liquid</li></ol>

***свистеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свистеть.html>свисте́ть</a> (5624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистеть.html>свисте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svistétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистнуть.html>сви́стнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whistle, to make a whistling sound <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with or without the aid of a whistle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистать.html>свиста́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only when made without the aid of a whistle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sing, to pipe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of birds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to whine <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a bullet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
